\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GlobalOptions}{GlobalOptions}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_global_options_tag}{Global\+Options\+Tag}} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_aba5e331f7bc533009ddbafbbe48deb82}{Global\+Options}}}

Structure for holding global options. This structure groups all the options that affect the text output into one structure.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void arc\+Box (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{ymin,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{ymax,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{box\+Start,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{box\+End,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_a726ea06e08404159bf4b7f6f1efbb03d}{Msc\+Arc\+Type}}}]{box\+Type,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{line\+Colour,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{bg\+Colour }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Draw vertical lines and boxes stemming from entities. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ymin} & Top of the row. \\
\hline
{\em ymax} & Bottom of the row. \\
\hline
{\em box\+Start} & Column in which the box starts. \\
\hline
{\em box\+End} & Column in which the box ends. \\
\hline
{\em box\+Type} & The type of box to draw, MSC\+\_\+\+ARC\+\_\+\+BOX, MSC\+\_\+\+ARC\+\_\+\+RBOX etc. \\
\hline
{\em line\+Colour} & Colour of the lines to use for rendering the box. \\
\hline
{\em bg\+Colour} & Background colour for rendering the box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{arcLine@{arcLine}!mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{arcLine()}{arcLine()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void arc\+Line (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_aca0247f7333b575de97470366d5b5c27}{Msc}}}]{m,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{y,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{ygradient,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{start\+Col,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{end\+Col,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Line\+Col,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__bool_8h_ae7d38601dfbd73adbe5c1b3ec34e0e13}{Boolean}}}]{has\+Arrows,  }\item[{const int}]{has\+Bi\+Arrows,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_a726ea06e08404159bf4b7f6f1efbb03d}{Msc\+Arc\+Type}}}]{arc\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Render the line and arrow head for some arc. This will draw the arc line and arrow head between two columns, noting that if the start and end column are the same, an arc is rendered. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & The Msc for which the text is being rendered. \\
\hline
{\em ymin} & Top of row. \\
\hline
{\em ymax} & Bottom of row. \\
\hline
{\em ygradient} & The gradient of the arc which alters the y position a the ending column. \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & Starting column for the arc. \\
\hline
{\em end\+Col} & Column at which the arc terminates. \\
\hline
{\em has\+Arrows} & If true, draw arc arrows, otherwise omit them. \\
\hline
{\em has\+Bi\+Arrows} & If true, has arrows in both directions. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Type} & The type of the arc, which dictates its rendered style. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{arcText()}{arcText()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void arc\+Text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_aca0247f7333b575de97470366d5b5c27}{Msc}}}]{m,  }\item[{FILE $\ast$}]{ismap,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{outwidth,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{ymid,  }\item[{int}]{ygradient,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{start\+Col,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{end\+Col,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{arc\+Label\+Line\+Count,  }\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{arc\+Label\+Lines,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Url,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Id\+Url,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Text\+Colour,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{arc\+Text\+Bg\+Colour,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_a726ea06e08404159bf4b7f6f1efbb03d}{Msc\+Arc\+Type}}}]{arc\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Render text on an arc. Draw the text on some arc. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & The Msc for which the text is being rendered. \\
\hline
{\em ismap} & If not {\itshape NULL}, write an ismap description here. \\
\hline
{\em outwidth} & Width of the output image. \\
\hline
{\em ymid} & Co-\/ordinate of the row on which the text should be aligned. \\
\hline
{\em start\+Col} & The column at which the arc being labelled starts. \\
\hline
{\em end\+Col} & The column at which the arc being labelled ends. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Label\+Line\+Count} & Count of lines of text in arc\+Label\+Lines. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Label\+Lines} & Array of lines of text from 0 to arc\+Label\+Line\+Count -\/ 1. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Url} & The URL for rendering the label as a hyperlink. This maybe {\itshape NULL} if not required. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Id} & The text identifier for the arc. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Id\+Url} & The URL for rendering the test identifier as a hyperlink. This maybe {\itshape NULL} if not required. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Text\+Colour} & Colour for the arc text, or NULL to use default. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Text\+Colour} & Colour for the arc text background, or NULL to use default. \\
\hline
{\em arc\+Type} & The type of arc, used to control output semantics. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{computeCanvasSize@{computeCanvasSize}!mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeCanvasSize()}{computeCanvasSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_row_info}{Row\+Info}} $\ast$ compute\+Canvas\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_aca0247f7333b575de97470366d5b5c27}{Msc}}}]{m,  }\item[{unsigned int $\ast$}]{w,  }\item[{unsigned int $\ast$}]{h }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Compute the output canvas size required for some MSC. This computes the dimensions for the canvas as well as the height for each row.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em m} & The MSC to analyse. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em w} & Pointer to be filled with the output width. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em h} & Pointer to be filled with the output height. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An array giving the height of each row. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_aeba6321dd352d150b3db89b5469be64c}\label{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_aeba6321dd352d150b3db89b5469be64c}} 
\index{mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}!computeLabelLines@{computeLabelLines}}
\index{computeLabelLines@{computeLabelLines}!mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeLabelLines()}{computeLabelLines()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static unsigned int compute\+Label\+Lines (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_aca0247f7333b575de97470366d5b5c27}{Msc}}}]{m,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__msc_8h_a726ea06e08404159bf4b7f6f1efbb03d}{Msc\+Arc\+Type}}}]{arc\+Type,  }\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$$\ast$}]{lines,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{label,  }\item[{int}]{start\+Col,  }\item[{int}]{end\+Col }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Split an input arc label into lines, word-\/wrapping if needed. This takes the literal label supplied from the input and splits it into an array of char $\ast$ text lines. Splitting is first done according to literal \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{} character sequences added by the user, then according to word wrapping to fit available space, if appropriate.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em m} & The MSC for which the lines are to be split. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em arc\+Type} & The type of the arc being labelled. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em lines} & Pointer to be filled with output line array. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em label} & Original arc label from input file. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em start\+Col} & Column in which the arc starts. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em end\+Col} & Column in which the arc ends, or -\/1 for broadcast arcs.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The returned strings and array must be free()\textquotesingle{}d. \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_a3d0b5aeb109aefd7ba3c4fe25bb76f9b}{free\+Label\+Lines()}} can be used for this purpose. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getLine()}{getLine()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static char $\ast$ get\+Line (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{string,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{line,  }\item[{char $\ast$const}]{out,  }\item[{const unsigned int}]{out\+Len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Get some line from a string containing \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{} delimiters. Given a string that contains literal \textquotesingle{}~\newline
\textquotesingle{} delimiters, return a subset in a passed buffer that gives the nth line.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em string} & The string to parse. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em line} & The line number to return from the string, which should count from 0. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em out} & Pointer to a buffer to fill with line data. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em out\+Len} & The length of the buffer pointed to by {\itshape out}, in bytes. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} pointer to {\itshape out}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acdd38206d295f4257eb1768061c5ef9c}\label{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acdd38206d295f4257eb1768061c5ef9c}} 
\index{mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}!splitStringToWidth@{splitStringToWidth}}
\index{splitStringToWidth@{splitStringToWidth}!mscgen\_api.c@{mscgen\_api.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{splitStringToWidth()}{splitStringToWidth()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static char $\ast$ split\+String\+To\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2mscgen__api_8c_acb0c412e6e9446bdd2f952dc9ee707bd}{Context}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{l,  }\item[{unsigned int}]{width }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Word wrap a line of text until the first line is less than {\itshape width} wide. This removes words from the input line and builds them into a 2nd new string until the input line is shorter than the supplied width. The input string is directly truncated, while the remaining characters are returned in a new memory allocation. On return, the input line of text will be shorter than {\itshape width}, while the newly returned string will contain all the remaining characters.

If the input line is already shorter than {\itshape width}, the function returns NULL and does not modify the input line of text.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em l} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_input}{Input}} line of text which maybe modified if needed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em width} & Maximum allowable text line width. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
NULL if {\itshape l} was already less then {\itshape width} long, otherwise a new string giving the remained of the string. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
